<div id="review_371848698" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/371848698" />
    <a title="Leigh Collazo" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/4141951-leigh-collazo"><img alt="Leigh Collazo" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1589123295p2/4141951.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/371848698?book_show_action=true">Jul 18, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Leigh Collazo" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Leigh Collazo" href="/user/show/4141951-leigh-collazo">Leigh Collazo</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was ok"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was ok</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4141951-leigh-collazo?shelf=net-galley">net-galley</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4141951-leigh-collazo?shelf=pub-date-2012">pub-date-2012</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4141951-leigh-collazo?shelf=read-in-2012">read-in-2012</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer371848698" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer13876703671088864333"><br/>More reviews from <a href='http://readerpants.blogspot.com' rel='nofollow noopener'>Mrs. ReaderPants</a>.<br/><br/><b>REVIEW:</b> Sigh. With all the glowing reviews I've seen on Goodreads, I had high hopes for this one. Poorly-paced with boring characters and plenty of melodrama, <i>Time Between Us</i> was "okay" at best and royally irritating at worst. I didn't hate it, but I didn't really like it, either. I thought about abandoning it several times, but I stuck it out because of the glowing reviews. If you are currently reading it and love it, then please carry on and ignore my review.</span>
  <span id="freeText13876703671088864333" style="display:none"><br />More reviews from <a href="http://readerpants.blogspot.com" rel="nofollow noopener">Mrs. ReaderPants</a>.<br /><br /><b>REVIEW:</b> Sigh. With all the glowing reviews I've seen on Goodreads, I had high hopes for this one. Poorly-paced with boring characters and plenty of melodrama, <i>Time Between Us</i> was "okay" at best and royally irritating at worst. I didn't hate it, but I didn't really like it, either. I thought about abandoning it several times, but I stuck it out because of the glowing reviews. If you are currently reading it and love it, then please carry on and ignore my review. But if you are reading it, wondering at the glowing reviews and thinking "surely it gets better," take my word for it: it doesn't. A few things I didn't like:<br /><br />Nice-but-boring characters. The four major characters are all perfectly pleasant people who I might know or like in real life, but for a novel about something as exciting as time-travel, none of them seem interesting enough.<br /><br />"It's all about Anna." It feels that way, anyways. I do appreciate that Anna has a life of her own separate from Bennett. She has multiple friends, a passion for running, supportive parents, and a bright future, so I never really understood her obsession with travel and worry over "being stuck" in her small town. Really, girl? You are only in high school; most people haven't done lots of traveling in high school. Her hopelessness that she'll "never leave this town" is completely silly. Doesn't she realize that after high school, it's all up to her? She's a spring-semester senior graduating in a few weeks--what does she think happens after graduation? Methinks she doesn't have as much "fight" as her friend Emma gives her credit for.<br /><br />Drama. While Anna has plenty to keep herself busy, Bennett is a lot less involved in his own life and seems to live only for Anna. He's ready to leave his whole life, family, time period behind for some chick he's barely known a month. Most teen boys in a new relationship would run the other way if their new girlfriend got all pouty and dramatic the way Anna does. She really rakes him over the coals at times, all because he didn't tell her "everything." Get over yourself, Anna. <br /><br />Sketchy details. I also questioned the premise behind Bennett's whole ability to time-travel. Seriously? He just decided one day to think about another place and time, and it worked? No other explanation? No time travelers in the family? No freak industrial accident? No ancient time-traveling rock? Nothing?<br /><br />Slow pacing. With only one real conflict, <i>Time Between Us</i> barely had enough substance to sustain an entire novel. I didn't really care if Anna and Bennett could make their romance work, and I thought the stuff with Emma (if you've read it, you know what I'm talking about) missed a huge opportunity for a cool secondary (or even primary) storyline. I was more interested in the fallout of the Emma/Justin storyline than I was in the romantic outcome of two nice-but-uninteresting people. How disappointing that the story didn't better explore Emma's change of fate or the repercussions of screwing around with time.<br /><br />I will say that I LOVED the abundant 90s music references, especially the lyrics to "If I Could" by Phish near the end of the story. I haven't thought about that song in forever, and I had to sing the lyrics over and over in my head to even remember it at all. Stone only includes the first few lines of the song, and it near about drove me crazy trying to remember the artist and title. <i>Hoist</i> was one of my favorite albums in college, and I had forgotten all about it. <br /><br />Since I didn't really care for it and gave all kinds of bad vibes in my review, I think it is only fair here to include some the many positive reviews I've read. Here are two:<br /><br /><a href="http://astormofwords.net/2012/06/29/time-between-us-by-tamara-ireland-stone/" rel="nofollow noopener">Review from A Storm of Words</a><br /><a href="http://shiploadofwilco.blogspot.com/2012/06/time-between-us-by-tamara-ireland-stone.html" rel="nofollow noopener">Review from A Shot in the Arm</a><br /><br /><b>THE BOTTOM LINE:</b> All in all, just okay. I've seen loads of positive reviews, so maybe it's just me. I don't think the book was <i>bad</i>, but I don't understand all the rave reviews, either.<br /><br /><b>STATUS IN MY LIBRARY:</b> It's not yet released, so we don't have it right now. I may still get it, especially if students request it or it becomes very popular. <br /><br /><b>READALIKES:</b> <i>Before I Fall</i> (Oliver); <i>The Time Traveler's Wife</i> (Niffenegger); <i>Twilight</i> (Meyer) <br /><br /><b>RATING BREAKDOWN:</b> <br /> 
  <br />
   Overall: 2/5 
  <br />
   Creativity: 3/5 
  <br />
   Characters: 2/5 
  <br />
   Engrossing: 2/5  
  <br />
   Writing: 3/5 
  <br />
   Appeal to teens: 4/5 
  <br />
   Appropriate length to tell the story: 3/5 
  <br />
 <br /><br /><b>CONTENT: </b> <br /> 
  <br />
   Language: none 
  <br />
    Sexuality: medium--some kissing, nondescript references to "spending the night"  
  <br />
   Violence: mild--a foiled robbery at knifepoint 
  <br />
    Drugs/Alcohol: none 
  <br />
 <br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="13876703671088864333" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<div id="review_261301992" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/261301992" />
    <a title="Anna (Literary Exploration)" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/4645069-anna-literary-exploration"><img alt="Anna (Literary Exploration)" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1578931083p2/4645069.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/261301992?book_show_action=true">Jan 13, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Anna (Literary Exploration)" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Anna (Literary Exploration)" href="/user/show/4645069-anna-literary-exploration">Anna (Literary Exploration)</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4645069-anna-literary-exploration?shelf=magical-realism">magical-realism</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4645069-anna-literary-exploration?shelf=time-travel">time-travel</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4645069-anna-literary-exploration?shelf=romance">romance</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer261301992" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer9148103630382216035">More of my reviews can be found on my blog: <a href='http://www.literaryexploration.com' rel='nofollow noopener'>Literary Exploration</a><br/><br/>When I first found out about Time Between Us I was so excited. Not only is the main character's name, Anna (like me!!), but time travel?! Yes please! I've even had the pleasure of meeting Tamara at a few local events, since she's a local author, so I was incredibly excited to dive in. Not only are the characters amazingly real, but the story itself is breathtaking. It definitely reminded me of The Time Traveler's Wife which is one o</span>
  <span id="freeText9148103630382216035" style="display:none">More of my reviews can be found on my blog: <a href="http://www.literaryexploration.com" rel="nofollow noopener">Literary Exploration</a><br /><br />When I first found out about Time Between Us I was so excited. Not only is the main character's name, Anna (like me!!), but time travel?! Yes please! I've even had the pleasure of meeting Tamara at a few local events, since she's a local author, so I was incredibly excited to dive in. Not only are the characters amazingly real, but the story itself is breathtaking. It definitely reminded me of The Time Traveler's Wife which is one of my most favorite books ever, and a little bit of The Lake House. Yes, two amazing stories that also involve romance and time travel. If you're a big fan of romance and time travel then you will definitely want to pick up a copy of Time Between Us!!<br /><br />I absolutely loved the characters in this story. Anna is strong, independent, intelligent, and driven. There is definitely a point where Bennett and Anna are struggling to hold on to each other, but I loved how Anna didn't curl up into a ball in the woods and cry about it for months. She really shows how strong she's become throughout the story. And Bennett... oh my God Bennett... If there was every a swoon-tastic boy in a YA story it's Bennett. He's so caring and romantic and I loved getting to know all of his secrets at the same time as Anna. Their relationship is definitely not normal, considering he travels through time, but it's romantic and easy to relate to. We can all remember out first loves :)<br /><br />The story itself is just fantastic. There are so many details that make this story so wonderful. Tamara's writing style is just gorgeous. She has a way with words that really helped paint a picture of certain settings. When Anna and Bennett go rock climbing, I seriously felt like I was scaling the mountain myself. Even the dialogue is great and so true to teenagers and the way they speak. There are even a couple plot twists that I had no idea were coming! By the end I was laughing and crying!<br /><br />Overall, I absolutely loved Time Between Us. It's an amazing story of love, loss, and friendship and I loved every minute of it. The characters are all amazing and easy to relate to, and I loved their growth throughout the book. If you haven't already added Time Between Us to your TBR do so NOW. I'm not sure if this book is a standalone, but I'm really hoping Tamara will write more of Anna and Bennett's story because I just couldn't get enough!!</span>
  <a data-text-id="9148103630382216035" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_1443460881" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1443460881" />
    <a title="Markéta" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/27285612-mark-ta"><img alt="Markéta" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1477644048p2/27285612.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1443460881?book_show_action=true">Nov 15, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Markéta" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Markéta" href="/user/show/27285612-mark-ta">Markéta</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/27285612-mark-ta?shelf=young-adult">young-adult</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/27285612-mark-ta?shelf=supernatural">supernatural</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1443460881" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer7625218547923182707"><b>4 stars!****</b><br/><br/>TIME BETWEEN US was a cross between Time traveller's wife and Jumper with bit of Butterfly Effect thrown into it.<br/><br/>Bennett can jump from one place to another and he can also travel in time as long as he was alive at that time. <br/><br/>Anna lives in 1995, she has an intense need inside of her - she wants to travel the world. She craves an adventure. Her monotonous life is interupted when a new student comes. Bennett is bit weird. He has way too long hair and he doesn't really want to socialize.</span>
  <span id="freeText7625218547923182707" style="display:none"><b>4 stars!****</b><br /><br />TIME BETWEEN US was a cross between Time traveller's wife and Jumper with bit of Butterfly Effect thrown into it.<br /><br />Bennett can jump from one place to another and he can also travel in time as long as he was alive at that time. <br /><br />Anna lives in 1995, she has an intense need inside of her - she wants to travel the world. She craves an adventure. Her monotonous life is interupted when a new student comes. Bennett is bit weird. He has way too long hair and he doesn't really want to socialize.<br /><br />Those two are drawn to each other. Not even his secret can keep them apart.<br /><br />I really enjoyed this book. It kept me on my toes to the last sentence. It was funny, witty, readable and gripping.<br /><br />I didn't like Anna's friends. At all. They were annoying and too damn selfish. I couldn't stand them and I'm glad that they weren't there for a long periods of time.<br /><br />It conveys a message. That even if you would have the chance to change some major or even minor parts of history, you shouldn't. Because even one tiny change can turn out to be a huge mistake. It could result in something much was worse. <b>Even if it sounds as a cliché - things do happen for a reason.</b> <br /><br />I still don't really understand how the whole thing worked. There was no explanation. There's a lot of hows, whos and whys unanswered but I'm quite okay with that. It fits the whole mood of the book.<br /><br />For more reviews visit <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://do-notdiewondering.blogspot.com">http://do-notdiewondering.blogspot.com</a></span>
  <a data-text-id="7625218547923182707" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

    <a title="Colleen Houck" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/1163228-colleen-houck"><img alt="Colleen Houck" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1425326771p2/1163228.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2121386790?book_show_action=true">Sep 18, 2017</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Colleen Houck" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Colleen Houck" href="/user/show/1163228-colleen-houck">Colleen Houck</a>
      </span>

          added it




        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1163228-colleen-houck?shelf=secrets">secrets</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1163228-colleen-houck?shelf=romance">romance</a>,

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1163228-colleen-houck?shelf=contemporary">contemporary</a>,

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2121386790" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer8355842318009978219">It's rare for me to add a contemporary book to my list of recommendations and, yes, I know, this one isn't strictly contemporary. There's an element of magic to it. I love the sweet romance. It reminds me of the movie Somewhere in Time with Christopher Reeve and Jane Seymour and if you haven't seen that one yet, add it to your list of movies to watch. Picked up book two immediately. </span>

          </span>

          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer162491911" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer1109757699431236826">What happens if you meet and fell in love with a boy who you should have never meet?????<br/>Anna and Bennett where never surppose to meet she is Sixteen living in Chicago in 1995. He is Seventeen living in San Fancissco in 2012.<br/><br/><br/>Anna and Bennett's story is a pure pleasure to read. Tamara Ireland Stone hooked me in to her amazing time traveling love story and broke my heart within the first three pages and I didn't stop reading til the end.<br/><br/>The relonship between Anna and Bennett is touching and shows h</span>
  <span id="freeText1109757699431236826" style="display:none">What happens if you meet and fell in love with a boy who you should have never meet?????<br />Anna and Bennett where never surppose to meet she is Sixteen living in Chicago in 1995. He is Seventeen living in San Fancissco in 2012.<br /><br /><br />Anna and Bennett's story is a pure pleasure to read. Tamara Ireland Stone hooked me in to her amazing time traveling love story and broke my heart within the first three pages and I didn't stop reading til the end.<br /><br />The relonship between Anna and Bennett is touching and shows how well Stone can write and tell a story to its fullness.<br /><br />I loved Anna's voice with in the book. I felt everything along with her and fell in love with Bennett too. Bennett is defo a swoon YA book boy that all girls (old or young) will fall in love with. <br /><br />Bennett has rules for his time traveling three of them being <br />-Never to change an event that has happened<br />-Never to travel out of his life time<br />-Never tell anyone he can time travel<br /><br />But he has broken all of the above rules. He broke one for his sister Brooke and she is lost in that time still. He is searching for her which is how Anna meets him. The other two rules he breaks for Anna first when he tells her about himself and then he changes an event that had a big effect of her best friend Emma and her boyfriend Justin.<br /><br />I was so invested in this book I cried when Bennett takes Anna to his time in 2012 and she gets ripped away from him and you see Anna stugle to cope and then move on after him leaving. You really have that felling that oh no what happens if there never make it back to each other. <br /><br />Time Between Us has been on my book wish-list since April 2011 and what can I say the wait was totally worth it. I loved every single second the romance,time travel,side characters and the dates between Anna and Bennett.<br /><br />Time Between Us is a book that I wish I could just quote all of it because I love it so much but I can't so here are my top 6 quotes.<br /><br />-"I close my eyes as his thumb slides toward my mouth and brushes my lower lip, and I can feel myself moving in closer, like I'm being pulled in to the gravity that surrounds him."<br /><br />-"I don't stay anywhere.I vist.I observe.I leave.I don't ever stay."<br /><br />-"I spent most of the night distracted by a time traveler who vists but never stays. An incredible,beautiful boy with eyes I can never seem to get out of my head."<br /><br />-"As I look around the forest with sunlight gleaming through the sky, unlike Ko Tao, I can always come back here when he's gone. When I'm missing him, like I already know I will be."<br /><br />-"I know I'm supposed to care, but I don't, not right now. I don't want to think about what he can do and where he go and when he might leave, because at this momentwe're both in the exact same place at the exact same time."<br /><br />-"I'm saying....I'm completely in love with you. And I guess I'm wondering...What if Ididn't leave after all?"<br /><br />Time Between Us is a must read for any YA fan a amazing 2012 debut with a rocking cover.</span>

<div id="review_281861868" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/281861868" />
    <a title="Margie" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/7258173-margie"><img alt="Margie" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1508384117p2/7258173.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/281861868?book_show_action=true">Feb 21, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Margie" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Margie" href="/user/show/7258173-margie">Margie</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer281861868" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer4358197012638804798">Such an original and believable time-travel-love story! <br/><br/>Bennett travels through time, and usually he does it for fum. But this time, there is a reason he has to go back, and ends up in Anna's time. As much as he tries to stay away, tries to remain unnoticed by all so he doesn't disturb "history", is there a possibility that things happened for a reason? Was he meant to come here? To meet her? <br/>Anna goes to a private school where everyone is the majority of the students are privileged own cars and</span>
  <span id="freeText4358197012638804798" style="display:none">Such an original and believable time-travel-love story! <br /><br />Bennett travels through time, and usually he does it for fum. But this time, there is a reason he has to go back, and ends up in Anna's time. As much as he tries to stay away, tries to remain unnoticed by all so he doesn't disturb "history", is there a possibility that things happened for a reason? Was he meant to come here? To meet her? <br />Anna goes to a private school where everyone is the majority of the students are privileged own cars and have traveled plenty. Anna is okay with the fact that her parents both have to work overtime in order to put through her school to give her the best education and she is all prepared to start her senior year, with the hopes to travel once she graduates. It is something that she has always wanted to do and fears that she may not be able to because of her lack of finances... but in the end, life is good for Anna. <br />When she meets Bennett, its hard to say how she feels about him. And as she bumps into him and little by little gets to know him, she is not sure what to think of him. They're relationship slowly unfolds... she continuously feels that that Bennett may be hiding things; that he may not be telling her everything... can she trust him? <br /><br />I really loved seeing how independent Anna was! Even after meeting Bennett and the things they went through, she did not completely crumble but got herself together and became stronger. <br />Oh my, and Bennett... you will fall in love with this boy! Other than the fact that he is a time traveler, he is still such a unique and memorable character. He is not perfect, but no boy ever is. But he makes up for it, in so many ways. <br /><br />As a teen who grew up in the early 90's (oh my, did I just give away my age?!), who was in high school when Kurt Cobain passed away and who thought that Eddie Vedder (of Pearl Jam) was a god - all of the 90's references brought me back in time as well! I felt like I was 16, 17, 18 all over again, which makes me love this book even more!<br /><br />And it has to be said, I really enjoyed this so much more than The Time Travelers Wife, which was much more serious and at times lagged - Time Between Us picks up after about 100 pages or so and then it has you continuously turning the pages! You won't be able to put it down - so be careful you don't get any paper-cuts!</span>
  <a data-text-id="4358197012638804798" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

              <span id="reviewTextContainer319831403" class="readable"

<span id="freeTextContainer4734753409693364983">4.5 stars!! <br/><br/>I can admit it... I haven't really read a lot of time travel books, so I was a bit leery going into this. I don't know what I was thinking. I absolutely loved it. <br/><br/>Anna lives in 1995 in Chicago.<br/><br/>Bennett lives in 2012 in San Francisco.<br/><br/>They were never supposed to meet.<br/><br/>Bennett has an incredible ability to travel through time. There are a few catches to the whole process, but as long as he stays within the years he's been alive, he's never had any trouble, and I thought this was a wonderfu</span>
  <span id="freeText4734753409693364983" style="display:none">4.5 stars!! <br><br>I can admit it... I haven't really read a lot of time travel books, so I was a bit leery going into this. I don't know what I was thinking. I absolutely loved it. <br><br>Anna lives in 1995 in Chicago.<br><br>Bennett lives in 2012 in San Francisco.<br><br>They were never supposed to meet.<br><br>Bennett has an incredible ability to travel through time. There are a few catches to the whole process, but as long as he stays within the years he's been alive, he's never had any trouble, and I thought this was a wonderful twist to the story. <br><br>He shows up in Chicago in 1995, seemingly out of nowhere. Anna first encounters him on the bleachers while she runs one morning, only Bennett says it wasn't him. The bulk of the story takes place during this time period and it was wonderful to relive all the things that were going on back then... the music references and concerts!<br><br>After something happens that forces Bennett to spill his secrets to Anna, they grow closer. I couldn't help but feel nervous for these two, simply because Bennett was somewhere he wasn't supposed to be and Anna was falling for him completely. <br><br><i>I'm not sure what I'm supposed to do with this information. Tell him to leave? Tell him to stay? But I don't have time to consider any other alternatives, because he scoots in closer and brings his hands to my face, and I fall back into the bookcase as he kisses me with this intensity-like he wants to be here, and if he kisses me just long enough, deeply enough, none of what he just said will actually be true. And as much as I know it's all true and that it's incredibly stupid to feel this way about someone who doesn't belong here-who, when he leaves, will hardly be a plane ride away-my hands leave the Berber carpet, find his back, and pull him toward me until I'm flat against the shelves. Because he's here now. And because I'm pretty certain I don't want this to stop. Ever.</i><br><br><a href="http://s757.beta.photobucket.com/user/jaimearkin/media/tumblr_m1csnkIFlC1rn95k2o1_250.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380376200ra/730986.gif" alt="Photobucket" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>After something happens and both Bennett and Anna test his abilities by changing the past and breaking his personal rules for his ability, I swear I read with a ball of nerves resting in my stomach, waiting for something to happen. I mean, they are messing with fate and I've seen that movie The Butterfly Effect. Just saying. <br><br>I really enjoyed the characters - definitely Anna, while I found myself a bit angry with her a few times, I thought she was written really well. I did find myself emotionally attached to her and her feelings so she obviously worked for me.<br><br>Bennett, once we got to know him was sweet and protective and caring and while their relationship wasn't born of the normal, he made the effort to try and give her the normal as well as the spectacularly grand and unbelievable. <br><br>One thing I would have liked to know more about is the manifestation of his ability. We get a brief explanation, which works for the book, but being naturally curious you wonder if there is anyone else like him, who has this talent as well ... where did it come from, why him... those kinds of things. I myself would have a hard time accepting the ability without doing tons of digging and trying to find out why me. <br><br>I also would have liked to know what happened with Anna in her previous life... why in the prologue does she give him the letter and what made her first choice not the right one for her. <br><br>I think what is most intriguing about this book is the idea of time travel itself and changing history... 'what if' ... what if you could have made a different choice in life, what if you could change the outcome of an event. All these things are intriguing and can't help but make you as a reader think of the way things might be different in your life if only...<br><br>Once I started this book it was hard to put down, like I said, I turned page after page nervous for these two while reading. If you're looking for a sweet contemporary YA romance than this is just the thing for you. <br><br>This review can be found on my blog, Fic Fare: <br><br><a href="http://fictionfare.blogspot.com/" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380223306ra/681029.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br></span>
  <a data-text-id="4734753409693364983" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<span id="freeTextContainer5088065007306441438">I want to time travel to 2012 just so I can squee with more people about TIME BETWEEN US! It's a sweet romantic journey perfect for curling up with under the covers and losing yourself. In full disclosure, I am friends with Tamara Ireland Stone, but that simply gives me another reason to love her book even more! <br/><br/>Anna Greene has dreamed of traveling her whole life, but she's barely left the borders of her home state, Illinois. She knows there's something mysterious about Bennett Cooper when she m</span>
  <span id="freeText5088065007306441438" style="display:none">I want to time travel to 2012 just so I can squee with more people about TIME BETWEEN US! It's a sweet romantic journey perfect for curling up with under the covers and losing yourself. In full disclosure, I am friends with Tamara Ireland Stone, but that simply gives me another reason to love her book even more! <br /><br />Anna Greene has dreamed of traveling her whole life, but she's barely left the borders of her home state, Illinois. She knows there's something mysterious about Bennett Cooper when she meets him, and as their romance unfolds, Anna will travel to places she's never thought possible. <br /><br />I really loved the chemistry between Anna and Bennett, but the romance was well balanced with a touch of mystery and adventure. Anna finds herself on a heart-pounding journey at home AND away, while having to confront serious choices and consequences in her personal life. The decisions she makes are heart-wrenching and believable. I couldn't stop turning pages to find out What Happens Next?!<br /><br />If I'm being a *little* vague, it's because I don't want to spoil anything before the book comes out! Simply put, TIME BETWEEN US was well crafted, a lot of fun, and will grab you by the heart strings and take you on an amazing journey! </span>

<div id="review_434374601" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/434374601" />
    <a title="Sarah" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/4096145-sarah"><img alt="Sarah" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1431452621p2/4096145.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/434374601?book_show_action=true">Oct 14, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Sarah" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Sarah" href="/user/show/4096145-sarah">Sarah</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Audiobook 9780307967879" href="/book/show/13573048-time-between-us">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4096145-sarah?shelf=audiobook">audiobook</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer434374601" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer10248589929655239275">My extended review is on Clear Eyes, Full Shelves - <a target='_blank' rel='noopener nofollow' href='http://cleareyesfullshelves.com/blog/review-time-between-us'>http://cleareyesfullshelves.com/blog/...</a><br/><br/>So, I'm definitely onboard for the sequel, because there's something that sucks you in with this story. It's engaging and definitely entertaining and twisty regarding the plot. <br/><br/>HOWEVER...<br/><br/>The is much in this story that's problematic:<br/><br/>1) The time-travel aspect is weaksauce. There are few "rules" to the time travel beyond that it's a bad idea to alter the past and that you can only travel within your own life</span>
  <span id="freeText10248589929655239275" style="display:none">My extended review is on Clear Eyes, Full Shelves - <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://cleareyesfullshelves.com/blog/review-time-between-us">http://cleareyesfullshelves.com/blog/...</a><br /><br />So, I'm definitely onboard for the sequel, because there's something that sucks you in with this story. It's engaging and definitely entertaining and twisty regarding the plot. <br /><br />HOWEVER...<br /><br />The is much in this story that's problematic:<br /><br />1) The time-travel aspect is weaksauce. There are few "rules" to the time travel beyond that it's a bad idea to alter the past and that you can only travel within your own lifetime. Frankly, the time-travel stuff is more like random paranormalcy than time-travel. At one point Bennett does math to figure out how to alter a timeline without causing a ripple effect and I was just, "Guys, you need more than a little algebra to pull that off. You'll better call Peter and Walter Bishop to make this happen."<br /><br />2) The set-up of Anna's school/home life is nonsensical. Her parents scrimp so she can attend a fancy private school in Evanston, where they live. This means that she has to get a running scholarship to afford college and won't ever be able to travel, which has been her dream since childhood. It's not as if Evanston, Ill has the world's worst public schools and her education would suffer by attending a public school and therefore enabling her parents to save for college and possibly a study abroad or exchange program. Torpedoing their child's college and life dreams in order to pay for a private high school doesn't make a lot of sense and besides this perplexing problem, makes no sense, as Anna's parents are generally great people who love their daughter and have a good relationship with her. Plus, there were no plot circumstances that required she need to attend that school. <br /><br />3) Anna is pretty passive about her own life's course. And while I get that she's a teen, and that's one of the things that kind of happens to teens, the fact that she's so passionate about running and travel, her passivity felt incongruous. <br /><br />4) I wanted to know more about Bennett and his backstory. I understand the sequel will be told from his POV, and I think that's a good thing. He also makes some decisions which I felt were not his to make, and I didn't know enough about him to understand if those decisions were justifiable or not.<br /><br />5) Anna's kind of a crappy friend and it really doesn't make a lot of sense, because she has two wonderful friends in Emma and Justin.<br /><br />6) I never bought that the thing Anna and Bennett changed in their timeline could have been down without changing more than the one--ultimately not that significant--thing that they changed. I've watched enough Fringe to understand the damn Butterfly Effect, y'all.<br /><br />7) I started counting the number of times Anna thought something along the lines of, "I let out a breath I didn't know I was holding." Girl, just breath, all right?<br /><br />Anyway, I know it sounds like I hated this book, and I actually really enjoyed it, despite the problems with the plot holes and character motivation. While the beginning/setup drags a bit, it's generally well-paced and has a nice balance of action and romance-y stuff. This was definitely aided by the fact that I listened to the audiobook and the narrator did an excellent job not only with differentiating the voices, but building tension that I suspect would've been somewhat less had I read it as opposed to listening. </span>
  <a data-text-id="10248589929655239275" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_405474609" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/405474609" />
    <a title="Kayla" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/5696962-kayla"><img alt="Kayla" src="https://s.gr-assets.com/assets/nophoto/user/f_50x66-6a03a5c12233c941481992b82eea8d23.png" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/405474609?book_show_action=true">Jan 15, 2018</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Kayla" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Kayla" href="/user/show/5696962-kayla">Kayla</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5696962-kayla?shelf=reviews-completed">reviews-completed</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5696962-kayla?shelf=netgalley-and-edelweiss">netgalley-and-edelweiss</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer405474609" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer6834107175127460996">3.5 stars. <br/><br/>Recently I've gotten into reading stories about time travel. I don't know if it's from my obsessive Doctor Who watching or what, but it's all I've wanted to read about lately. Time Between Us has been on my tbr for a while, so I decided to give it a try. I went in with no expectations because I hadn't heard much about it, and ended up enjoying it, even though it was a little cliche.<br/><br/>At first, Time Between Us made me really confused, which I typically hate. However, it worked well in th</span>
  <span id="freeText6834107175127460996" style="display:none">3.5 stars. <br /><br />Recently I've gotten into reading stories about time travel. I don't know if it's from my obsessive Doctor Who watching or what, but it's all I've wanted to read about lately. Time Between Us has been on my tbr for a while, so I decided to give it a try. I went in with no expectations because I hadn't heard much about it, and ended up enjoying it, even though it was a little cliche.<br /><br />At first, Time Between Us made me really confused, which I typically hate. However, it worked well in this book. I liked finding out things alongside Anna, instead of just being told what was happening right away. It added to the mystery and suspense of the book, and kept me interested. There was a lot of mystery and intrigue throughout the book. When it was finally revealed when Bennett was born, my jaw dropped. It added a whole new layer to the story, which made things even more complex. I loved it.<br /><br />There are a few problems that I had with the book. It was very tropey, and cliche. It reminded me a lot of Twilight in a way, which might be good for it's intended young adult audience, but I've been over the whole Twilight thing for a few years now. I've outgrown it. For example, a lot of the important scenes take place in a school cafeteria, like Twilight. There's also an unexplainable connection to each other, and instalove that's similar to Twilight. Last but not least, he shows up uninvited her bedroom, which reminded me of Twilight, and is always creepy. The plot was also predictable at times. I guessed what was going to happen with the contest, and a few other things that I don't want to get too into because of spoilers, from the start. <br /><br />Even though I had a couple of issues with Time Between Us, I ended up really enjoying it. It made me want to read more of Tamara Ireland Stone's books, which I will be doing right away. I think it should be interesting to read the sequel to this, Time After Time. I'm not sure how a sequel will take place after the way everything ended, but I'm excited to read it because I really want more of these characters. I recommend this book for young adult readers, those that like Twilight and want similar books, and people that love reading about time travel.</span>
  <a data-text-id="6834107175127460996" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('w/J30SaVXqBJAdds831TyUytvfmQGHXN2qjj9HXf9+hOSITzeAYRMR6UIa7ikf2b6agg/ga/A3n4aSSu5p+/9A==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

<div class='bookAuthorProfile__about'>

<span id="freeTextContainer10635875006759796903">TAMARA IRELAND STONE spent nearly two decades in the technology industry before she began writing middle grade and young adult fiction. She feels lucky to say she's had two careers she's loved.<br/><br/>Her New York Times bestseller, EVERY LAST WORD, won the Cybils Young Adult Fiction Award, the Georgia Peach Book Award, and was a YALSA Teens' Top Ten pick; LITTLE DO WE KNOW won the NCIBA Golden Poppy Award</span>
  <span id="freeText10635875006759796903" style="display:none">TAMARA IRELAND STONE spent nearly two decades in the technology industry before she began writing middle grade and young adult fiction. She feels lucky to say she's had two careers she's loved.<br /><br />Her New York Times bestseller, EVERY LAST WORD, won the Cybils Young Adult Fiction Award, the Georgia Peach Book Award, and was a YALSA Teens' Top Ten pick; LITTLE DO WE KNOW won the NCIBA Golden Poppy Award for Young Adult Fiction; and her debut novel, TIME BETWEEN US, has been published in over twenty languages. The first book in her middle-grade series, CLICK'D, was a Sunshine State Young Readers Award pick, a Kids' Indie Next pick, a Cybils Award Nominee, and an NCIBA Golden Poppy nominee. <br /><br />Tamara is a proud nerd, vinyl collector, and movie lover. She burns everything she cooks. <br /><br />She lives in the San Francisco Bay Area.</span>
